 unhone salaami ballebaaj aar je nichol ko clin bold kar diya

 unhone 4 over main 31 ran kharchakar 3 wicket jatke

 jawaab main bhartiya team kharaab shuruyaat se ubarte hue shandaar vaapasi kii or viraat kohli (70) ke joardaar ardhashatak kii badaulat jeet ke kareeb pahunchi lekin behad naatakeey andaaj main use antim over main munh kii khaani padi
 The Indian team could manage only 166 runs after losing four wickets in 20 overs
 virendra sahvaag ke chotil hone kii vajah se gautam gambhir ke saath pari kii shuruyaat karne aae viraat kohli ne team india ko tej shuruyaat di

 The strike of resident doctors at Safdarjung Hospital has ended
 doctoron ne swasthya sachiv se milane ke baad yah faisla liya
 From Tuesday night at the Safdarjung Hospital, the patients had to face heavy problems due to the strike by the resident doctors
 der raat ek garbhvatee mahila ko yah kahkar lautaa diya gaya ki doctor uplabdh nahin hai
 Hospital emergency services are also affected
 gambhir rup se biimaar marijon ko aspataal se waapas lautnaa padaa
 It is worth mentioning that the resident doctors went on strike last week demanding regular salary payment, better hostel facilities and security, following which the Health Department assured to listen to their demands, but the striking doctors allege that so far No action has been taken on the demands
 doctoron kaa kahana he ki unki maangon par kya ection liya ja rahaa he, isaki likhit report unhen di jaae
 Patients are suffering because of the ongoing tussle between the hospital administration and the doctor

 Hardeep, who works in a news channel, was sitting in his house with friends
 uske flats ke neeche ek raisajade kaa gym tha
 a liquor party was going on in the gym, fast music was playing
 hardip ne neeche party kar rahe logon se shor na karne kaa nivaden kiya to raisajade ko ye baat bardaasht nahin hui or usne patrkaar ko goli maar di
 Hardeep was responsible for the entire family
 The incident is in the posh Vasant Kunj area of delhi
 vaardaat ravivaar kii he
 30-year-old Hardeep had worked in several news channels and was the only son of parents
 hardip ke ghar ke neeche rinku naam ke shaks kaa gym he or usee ke gym main raat ko lagbhag saadhe das baje sharaab party chal rahi thi
 When Hardeep told Rinku not to make noise, first he abused Hardeep
 uske baad hardip waapas apane kamare main aa gaya
 Shortly after reaching the hospital, Rinku reached the room of gun taunt Hardeep and shot him after hitting him
 iske baad rinku vahaan maujuud hardip ke doston ko dhamka bandook laharaata hua chalaa gaya
 Hardeep's friends called 100, but the police did not arrive
 dost unhen auto main baitaakar safadarajang aspataal le gaye or aspataal pahunchane ke kuch der baad hi hardip ne dam tod diya
 Hardeep's family lives in Kaithal, Haryana
 aaropee ab tak fararpulice ne hatya kaa maamla to darj kar liya he, lekin abhi tak aaropee rinku kigiraftaarnahin ho pai he
 Apart from us, many other small creatures live in our house
 kuch jeev aise hote hai jinke hone se hamen koi nuksaan nahin hota he lekin kuch aise bhi hote hai jinke hone se hamaara ghar ganda ho jaataa he
 Or they become the cause of some disease
 makadi ek aisa hi keet he jo ghar kii deevaaron, cono or andheri jagahon par jaala bunata he
 Usually these spiders do not cause any harm to people, but there are also some whose blisters on the open skin cause blisters at that place
 vaise to in makadiyon ko dur rakhane ke liye kai tarah ke kitnashak bazaar main uplabdh hai lekin hamamen se kuch logon ko lagata he ki kitnashak kaa istemaal unke or ghar ke duusare sadasyon ke swasthya ko prabhavit kar saktaa he
 But you might not know that spiders can be taken out of the house by adopting domestic methods
 1
 First of all clean the spider webs
 dhyaan se sabase pehle ghar ke baahar ke jaale saaf kiijie kyonki zyaadaatar makadiyaan ghar ke baahar hi apana jaala bunati hai
 The corners of the walls are the most suitable place to live
 2
 This is the easiest solution
 koshish kiijie ki aap ghar main safai karne ke dauraan ekbar deevaaren or chhipe hue konon ko acchhee tarah dekhakar saaf kar len
 By doing this, the fish will not be able to flourish
 3
 It is very important to make sure that there is no broken wall in your house
 na hi usamen daraaren hon
 Spiders thrive most in such places
 agar daraaren hai bhi to unhen turant se bhar den
 4
 sirka ek aisa padaarth he jo aise kiton ko martha to he lekin maanav swasthya par koi bura asar nahin daalata he
 If you wish, you can dip vinegar in a cloth and keep it in places where spiders are more likely to occur
 5
 Spiders also run away with the use of baking soda
 makadiyon ko isaki gandh pasand nahin hoti he jisaki vah se ve baking soda ke paas se bhaag jaati hai
 6
 citras oil ke istemaal se bhi makadiyaan ghar chhodkar bhaag jaati hai
 E-cigarettes are being made more prevalent with the idea of being less dangerous than old cigarettes, as it does not contain hazardous smoke, tar and carbon monoxide
 lekin i-cigarette se hone vaale dil or fefdon ke rog ke khatre saamne aa rahe hai
 The World Health Organization (WHO) has also demanded strict restrictions on e-cigarettes
 taaja shodh main yah baat saamne ai he ki i-cigarette kii lat ke shikaar log aam cigarette pine waalon se zyada cigarette pite hai, jisase cardiyak simpathyttic activity anderlin kaa str or oxidentive tanaav bad jaataa he, jiske bare main mana jaataa he ki yah dil kii samasyaon ke khatre badha detaa he

, the National President of the Indian Mandical Association (IMA)
 ke
 K
 agarwal or general secretary dow
 R
 en
 Tandon says that e-cigarettes can also lead to nicotine addiction
 band jagahon par nicotine ke vaashp zyada khatarnaak ho sakate hai
 There is currently no control over artificial flavor and chemical products
 gilikol or acetone bhi khatarnaak tatv hai jo karsinogen kaa kaaran ban sakate hai
 Even though there is no smoke in e-cigarettes, other people come in contact with it
 shodh main karsigence jaise formdihide, benzene or tambaakoo aadhaarit nritosemins is apratyaksh i-cigarette ke seven se paidaa hone kaa pataa chalaa he
 Dr
 agarwal bataate hai ki i-cigarette se cancer hone kaa khatra ek packet cigarette pine kii tulana main 5 se 15 guna hota he
 Some smokeless tobacco contains three to four times as much nicotine, which is capable of causing toxicity to the structure of the heart, and e-cigarettes do not prevent this danger
 tippaniyan He says that exchanging such cigarettes with each other can spread diseases with viruses such as TB, herpes and hepatitis
 kishoron main iske badhate prayog kii vajah se yah or bhi chintaa kaa vishay ban gaya he
 Nicotine can inhibit brain development, which can make it difficult to concentrate and makes it difficult to control anger
 dow
 Aggarwal says that e-cigarette is actually a tobacco product
 iske khataron ke bare main kai pramaan maujuud hai, isliye saavdhaanee jaruri he
 Smokers learn the techniques of quitting it and adopt the same techniques that are recognized
 jaise, gam paches vagairah

 After 90, for the first time in 1962 Lok Sabha elections were held on bjp's Dhoomtharas parliamentary seat in which Congress party had won a tremendous victory
 uske baad 1967, 1971 main bhi yahaan congress kaa paracham laharaaya
 The Bharatiya Lok Dal won the anti-incumbency wave in 1977, while the Congress came back here in 1984
 1989 main hua chunaav yahaan janata dal ke khate main gaya tha
 After Ramalhar, bjp's stronghold in the 90s, it has been the seat of the Bharatiya Janata Party since 1991 under Ramalhar
 1991, 1996, 1998, 1999 or 2004 main yahaan bijepi ne jeet darj kii
 During this period, Krishna Lal Diler of BJP was an MP from 1996-2004
 2009 main yahaan rashtriya lokdal ke ummidavaar ne jeet darj kii, haalanki tab ralod-bijepi kaa gathbandhan tha
 In 2014, bjp's Rajesh Kumar Diwakar registered a landslide victory from here
 pashchimi uttar pradesh kii mahatvapurn loksabhaa siton main se ek hathras muslim-jat votaron ke prabhaav vaali seat he
 That is why BJP-RLD continued to win here
 pichley chunavi aankadon ke anusaar, yahaan par kareeb 17 lakh se adhik matadaata hai, inamen se kareeb 9
 6 lakh male voters and 7
 8 lakh mahila matadaata hai

 2017 main hue vidhansabha chunaav main sirf sadabad main basapa ne jeet darj kii thi, jabaki baaki anya 4 siton par bijepi ne jhanda laharaaya tha

 ' People from Uttar Pradesh to West Bengal have shared information about themselves being safe using this Facebook 'safety Check' facility
 is seva ko pichley saal oktober main shuru kiya gaya tha
 The service issues an alert for people stranded in disaster-hit areas, in which people share notifications about their safety to their Facebook friends
 fasebuk ke sansthaapak mark jukerbarg ne apane ek post main kaha tha, ‘prakritik aapadaa ke samay samudaay kii madad karne ke liye ‘sefti check’ hamaara ek prayaas he

 ise banane kaa vichaar varsh 2011 main japan main ai tsunami ke baad aayaa tha
 Similarly, Google's 'person Finder' helps people in affected areas to be informed about their safety
 yahaan par aap google ke databes main se apano kii jaankaree ko dhund sakate hai yaa kisi ke bare main jaankaree ko saajha kar sakate hai taaki or log use dhund saken
 There are two options on this, 'I am looking for someone' (I am looking for someone) and second 'I have information about someone' (I have information)
 google kii yah suvidha nepal or bharat ke hompej par hi uplabdh he

 is suvidha ke tahat kisi ko khojane ke liye bharat or america main esemes se bhi jaankaree jutai ja sakati he

 Facebook founder Mark Zuckerberg said in one of his posts, 'safety check' is our effort to help the community in times of natural disasters
